seconds\")\n\t\t\t\t});\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\tjQuery('#'+vidId).append(vidLength);\n\t\t\t}\n\t);\n}\n</script>\n    \n    <p align=\"right\"><strong><a Rinpoche</a> is a Tibetan Buddhist scholar and meditator who for 30 years has overseen the spiritual activities of the worldwide network of 160-plus centers, projects and social services that form the Foundation for the Preservation of the Mahayana Tradition (FPMT) which he founded with Lama Thubten Yeshe.</p><p>Read <a href=\"http://fpmt.org/teachers/zopa/\" target=\"_self\">more about Lama Zopa margin-right: 20px;\"><h2><a href=\"/fpmt/charitable-activities/\" target=\"_self\">Charitable Activities</a></h2> \t<!-- START .posts-grid -->\n\t<div class=\"posts-grid clearfix isotope\" style=\"position: relative; overflow: hidden; height: 708px;\">\n\t<!-- BEGIN .image-post --><div class=\"post blog-post col-4 image-post isotope-item\" style=\"position: absolute; left: 0px; top: 0px;\"><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/charitable-activities/projects/ordained-sangha/daily-lunch-offered-for-2017-for-the-monks-of-idgaa-choizinling-mongolia/\" class=\"post-featured-image\" target=\"_self\"><img src=\"https://fpmt.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/18/daily-lunch-offered-for-2017-for-the-monks-of-idgaa-choizinling-mongolia/mongolia-2-1-540x358.jpg?x33127\" alt=\"\"></a><!-- START .blog-post-excerpt --><div class=\"blog-post-excerpt\"><span class=\"arrow-up\"></span><h2><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/charitable-activities/projects/ordained-sangha/daily-lunch-offered-for-2017-for-the-monks-of-idgaa-choizinling-mongolia/\" target=\"_self\">Daily Lunch Offered for 2017 for the Monks of Idgaa Choizinling, Mongolia</a></h2>The Supporting Ordained Sangha Fund offers sponsorship for daily lunch for the 57 monks studying at Idgaa Choizinling Dratsang in Mongolia. Recently US$9,000 was offered to cover all of 2017. Idgaa Choizinling was established in 2003 through FPMT Mongolia due ... <p style=\"text-align:right;font-style:italic;\"><a class=\"read-more\" href=\"http://fpmt.org/charitable-activities/projects/ordained-sangha/daily-lunch-offered-for-2017-for-the-monks-of-idgaa-choizinling-mongolia/\" target=\"_self\">read full article »</a></p></div><!-- END .blog-post-excerpt --><!-- START .blog-post-meta --><div class=\"blog-post-meta clearfix\"><a class=\"meta-post post-date\" original-title=\"\">18th April 2017</a><div class=\"from-the-blog-meta\"></div></div><!-- END .blog-post-meta --></div><!-- END .image-post -->\t</div>\n\t<!-- END .posts-grid -->\n\t</div><div style=\"float: left; margin-right: 20px;\"><h2><a href=\"/fpmt/community-news/\" target=\"_self\">FPMT Community News</a></h2> <!-- START .posts-grid --><div class=\"posts-grid clearfix isotope\" style=\"position: relative; overflow: hidden; height: 613px;\"><!-- BEGIN .image-post --><div class=\"post blog-post col-4 image-post isotope-item\" style=\"position: absolute; left: 0px; top: 0px;\"><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/fpmt-community-news/news-around-the-world/the-103rd-ganden-tripa-passes-away/\" class=\"post-featured-image\" target=\"_self\"><img src=\"https://fpmt.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/23/the-103rd-ganden-tripa-passes-away/gaden-tripa-540x368.jpg?x33127\" alt=\"\"></a><!-- START .blog-post-excerpt --><div class=\"blog-post-excerpt\"><span class=\"arrow-up\"></span><h2><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/fpmt-community-news/news-around-the-world/the-103rd-ganden-tripa-passes-away/\" target=\"_self\">The 103rd Ganden Tripa Passes Away</a></h2>We are saddened to share the news of the passing of the 103rd Ganden Tripa Jetsun Lobsang Tenzin Rinpoche, who died on April 21, 2017, at 11:45 p.m. in Delhi, India, after an illness. According to the Central Tibetan Administration, ... <p style=\"text-align:right;font-style:italic;\"><a class=\"read-more\" href=\"http://fpmt.org/fpmt-community-news/news-around-the-world/the-103rd-ganden-tripa-passes-away/\" target=\"_self\">read full article »</a></p></div><!-- END .blog-post-excerpt --><!-- START .blog-post-meta --><div class=\"blog-post-meta clearfix\"><a class=\"meta-post post-date\" original-title=\"\">23rd April 2017</a><div class=\"from-the-blog-meta\"></div></div><!-- END .blog-post-meta --></div><!-- END .image-post --></div><!-- END .posts-grid --></div></div></div><p>&nbsp;</p><div class=\"section clearfix\"> <div class=\"col-9\"> <a name=\"welcome\"></a><a href=\"/fpmt/\" target=\"_self\"><h1>What is the Foundation for the Preservation of the Mahayana Tradition?</h1></a><p></p><div id=\"tabs-911\" class=\"tabs_container\"><ul class=\"tabs\"><li class=\"active\"><a href=\"#tab-welcome\" target=\"_self\">Welcome</a></li><li><a href=\"#tab-willkommen\" target=\"_self\">Willkommen</a></li><li><a href=\"#tab-bienvenidos\" target=\"_self\">Bienvenidos</a></li><li><a href=\"#tab-bienvenue\" target=\"_self\">Bienvenue</a></li><li><a href=\"#tab-benvenuto\" target=\"_self\">Benvenuto</a></li><li><a href=\"#tab-%e6%ad%a1%e8%bf%8e%e8%92%9e%e8%87%a8%e6%88%91%e5%80%91%e7%9a%84%e7%b6%b2%e7%ab%99\" target=\"_self\">歡迎蒞臨我們的網站</a></li></ul><div class=\"tabs_contents\"> <div id=\"tab-welcome\" class=\"tab_content\" style=\"display: block;\"> The FPMT is an organization devoted to preserving and spreading Mahayana Buddhism worldwide by creating opportunities to listen, reflect, meditate, practice and actualize the unmistaken teachings of the Buddha and based on that experience spreading the Dharma to sentient beings. We provide integrated education through which people’s minds and hearts can be transformed into their highest potential for the benefit of others, inspired by an attitude of universal responsibility and service. We are committed to creating harmonious environments and helping all beings develop their full potential of infinite wisdom and compassion.&nbsp;Our organization is based on the Buddhist tradition of Lama Tsongkhapa of Tibet as taught to us by our founder, Lama Thubten Yeshe and our spiritual director, Lama Thubten Zopa Rinpoche. </div> <div id=\"tab-willkommen\" class=\"tab_content\" style=\"display: none;\"><p>Die Gesellschaft zur Erhaltung der Mahayana Tradition (FPMT) ist eine weltweite Organisation, die sich der Verbreitung des Mahayana-Buddhismus widmet. Sie schafft Voraussetzungen, damit Menschen die fehlerlosen Unterweisungen des Buddha hören, über sie nachdenken und meditieren, sie praktizieren und verwirklichen können; auf der Basis dieser Erfahrungen trägt sie zur Verbreitung des Dharma unter den fühlenden Wesen bei.</p><p>Inspiriert von einer inneren Haltung der universellen Verantwortung und des Dienstes am Nächsten bietet sie ganzheitliche Bildung an, durch die Geist und Herz der Menschen in ihr höchstes Potenzial verwandelt werden können, zum Wohle der anderen. Sie strebt die Entwicklung friedvoller Gemeinschaften an und möchte allen Wesen helfen, ihr Potenzial für grenzenlose Weisheit und grenzenloses Mitgefühl zu verwirklichen. Unsere Organisation basiert auf der buddhistischen Überlieferungslinie des Lama Tsongkhapa aus Tibet, wie sie von unserem Gründer Lama Thubten Yeshe, und unserem spirituellen Leiter, Lama Thubten Zopa Rinpoche, gelehrt wird.</p><ul><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/belgium/\" target=\"_self\">Belgien</a> »</li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/germany/\" target=\"_self\">Deutschland</a> »</li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/switzerland/\" target=\"_self\">Die Schweiz</a> »</li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/austria/\" target=\"_self\">Österreich</a> »</li></ul></div> <div id=\"tab-bienvenidos\" class=\"tab_content\" style=\"display: none;\"><p>La Fundación para la preservación de la tradición Mahayana (FPMT) se dedica a la transmisión de la tradición y valores budistas mahayana en todo el mundo a través de enseñanzas de budismo tibetano, meditación, servicio a la comunidad, centros de retiro y proyectos que preservan la tradición. La FPMT está basada en la tradición guelugpa de Lama Tsong Khapa del Tíbet, tal como nos han enseñado nuestro fundador, Lama Thubten Yeshe, y nuestro director espiritual, Lama Zopa Rimpoché.</p><p>A continuación puede ver una lista de los centros y sus páginas web en su lengua preferida.</p><ul><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/argentina/\" target=\"_self\">Argentina</a></li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/colombia/\" target=\"_self\">Colombia</a></li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/spain/\" target=\"_self\">España</a></li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/mexico/\" target=\"_self\">México</a></li></ul><p><span class=\"pdf\"><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/wp-content/uploads/enews/2017/fpmt/Noticias de la Oficina Internacional Marzo 2017.pdf?x33127\" target=\"_blank\">Noticias de la FPMT – Marzo 2017</a></span></p></div> <div id=\"tab-bienvenue\" class=\"tab_content\" style=\"display: none;\"><p>La Fondation pour la Préservation de la Tradition du Mahayana (FPMT) est une organisation consacrée à la transmission dans le monde entier de la tradition et des valeurs du bouddhisme du mahayana, par l’enseignement, la méditation, les œuvres à caractère social, les centres de retraite et les projets qui préservent la tradition. La FPMT est fondée sur la tradition guéloukpa de Lama Tsongkhapa du Tibet, telle qu’elle a été enseignée par notre fondateur Lama Thoubtèn Yéshé et notre directeur spirituel, Lama Zopa Rinpoché.</p><p>Visitez le site de notre <span class=\"outgoing\"><a href=\"http://www.traductionfpmt.info\" target=\"_blank\">Service de traduction</a></span> pour les traductions, conseils et nouvelles en français.</p><p>Voici une liste de centres et de leurs sites dans votre langue préférée</p><ul><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/france/\" target=\"_self\">La France</a></li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/switzerland/\" target=\"_self\">La Suisse</a></li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/french-polynesia/\" target=\"_self\">Polynésie française</a></li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/ile-de-la-reunion/\" target=\"_self\">Ile de la Reunion</a></li></ul><p><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/enews/2015/fpmt/avril15.html\" target=\"_blank\">Nouvelles du Bureau International de la FPMT – Avril 2015</a></p></div> <div id=\"tab-benvenuto\" class=\"tab_content\" style=\"display: none;\"><p>La Fondazione per la Preservazione della Tradizione Mahayana (FPMT), opera per diffondere in tutto il mondo i valori e la tradizione buddhista attraverso gli insegnamenti del buddhismo tibetano, la meditazione, i centri di ritiro, le attività a carattere sociale e vari progetti mirati a preservare la tradizione stessa. L’FPMT si basa sul lignaggio Gelugpa e sugli insegnamenti del maestro tibetano Lama Tzongkhapa così come sono stati trasmessi dal nostro fondatore Lama Thubten Yeshe e dal direttore spirituale, Lama Zopa Rinpoche.</p><p>Di seguito potete trovare un elenco dei centri e dei loro siti nella lingua da voi prescelta.</p><ul><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/italy/\" target=\"_self\">L’Italia</a></li></ul><p><span class=\"pdf\"><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/wp-content/uploads/enews/2012/fpmt/NL_12_04_ITA.pdf?x33127\" target=\"_blank\">FPMT News Aprile</a></span></p></div> <div id=\"tab-%e6%ad%a1%e8%bf%8e%e8%92%9e%e8%87%a8%e6%88%91%e5%80%91%e7%9a%84%e7%b6%b2%e7%ab%99\" class=\"tab_content\" style=\"display: none;\"><p>護持大乘法脈聯合會（簡稱「護聯會」） 立足於創辦人圖敦．耶舍喇嘛與導師梭巴仁波切所傳授的宗喀巴大師之格魯派傳統，藉由西藏佛教的教授、 共修、公益服務、閉關道場以及護持法脈的事業，在全球弘揚大乘佛教的教法與價值觀。</p><p>由此進入，可以查看護聯會有哪些道場、網頁使用你點選的語言。</p><ul><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/china/\" target=\"_self\">中國</a> »</li><li><a href=\"http://fpmt.org/centers/taiwan/\" target=\"_self\">臺灣</a> »</li></ul></div> </div></div> </div> <div class=\"col-3 last-column\"> <a href=\"http://fpmt.org/media/resources/dharma-dates/\" style=\"text-align: center; display: block;\" target=\"_self\"><h1>Today’s Date</h1></a><p></p><div id=\"todays_date\"><div class=\"font_11\" style=\"\"><div align=\"center\"><strong><a href=\"/media/resources/dharma-dates/\" target=\"_self\">Apr 24, 2017</a></strong>*</div><div align=\"center\" style=\"font-size:10px;font-weight:normal;color:#4A4848;\">[Tibetan Date 28th]</div><br>\t\t     <div class=\"h1_bold tibetan_date\">\t\t   <i>28</i></div>\t\t  UD-FW<br>\t\t  NCH NF<br>\t\t  Fire puja<br>\t   <a href=\"/media/resources/dharma-dates/dates-explained/\" target=\"_self\">Key to Abbreviations »</a><div align=\"center\" class=\"legal\" style=\"color:#BABABA;\"><br><a class=\"tooltip\" original-title=\"\">*India Standard Time<span>*According to Ven. Choden Rinpoche, one of Lama Zopa Rinpoche's teachers, observation of auspicious days should be according to the date in India, not the date in one's home country. Therefore, when Lama Zopa Rinpoche is not in India, Rinpoche celebrates Buddha Days and other auspicious dates according to the time in India.</span></a></div></div></div><style>\n.tibetan_date {display:none;}\n</style>\n<script language=\"javascript\" type=\"text/javascript\">\n\nvar sURL = \"/resources/calendar/2017/April.php\";\nvar str2 = \"\";\n\nfunction processData(data) {\n  // taking care of data\n\tvar currCal = data;\n\tvar currDay = '<span class=\"h1_bold\">24</span>';\n\tvar str1 = currCal.substring(currCal.indexOf(currDay));\n\tstr1 = str1.substring(currDay.length,str1.indexOf(\"</TD>\"))\n\tvar tibDay = str1.substring(str1.indexOf('tibetan_date'));\n\tvar tibDay = tibDay.substring(tibDay.indexOf('<I>') + 3,tibDay.indexOf('</I></div>'));\n\tvar tibDayTest\n\tvar strSuffix;\n\ttibDay = String(tibDay);\n\tstrSuffix = tibDay.substr(-(Math.min(tibDay.length, 2))) > 3 && tibDay.substr(-(Math.min(tibDay.length, 2))) < 21 ? \"th\" : [\"th\", \"st\", \"nd\", \"rd\", \"th\"][Math.min(Number(tibDay)%10, 4)];\n\tvar str2 = \"\";\n\tstr2 = '<div class=\"font_11\" style=\"\"><div align=\"center\"><strong><a href=\"/media/resources/dharma-dates/\">Apr 24, 2017</a></strong>*</div><div align=\"center\" style=\"font-size:10px;font-weight:normal;color:#4A4848;\">[Tibetan Date ' + tibDay + strSuffix + ']</div><br>' + str1 + '<a href=\"/media/resources/dharma-dates/dates-explained/\">Key to Abbreviations &raquo;</a><div align=\"center\" class=\"legal\" style=\"color:#BABABA;\"><br><a class=\"tooltip\">*India Standard Time<span>*According to Ven.
